<p>Haines
and
James
Shaw
also
perform
with
<a
href="/wiki/Broken_Social_Scene?qsrc=3044"
onmousedown="triggerActionLog('primaryContent','','center','click','primaryContent','','');"
title="Broken
Social
Scene">Broken
Social
Scene</a>.
Haines
featured
as
vocalist
on
BSS'
albums
<i><a
href="/wiki/You_Forgot_It_in_People?qsrc=3044"
onmousedown="triggerActionLog('primaryContent','','center','click','primaryContent','','');"
title="You
Forgot
It
in
People">You
Forgot
It
in
People</a></i>,
<i><a
href="/wiki/Bee_Hives?qsrc=3044"
onmousedown="triggerActionLog('primaryContent','','center','click','primaryContent','','');"
title="Bee
Hives">Bee
Hives</a></i>,
<i><a
href="/wiki/Broken_Social_Scene_(album)?qsrc=3044"
onmousedown="triggerActionLog('primaryContent','','center','click','primaryContent','','');"
title="Broken
Social
Scene
(album)">Broken
Social
Scene</a></i>
and
<i><a
href="/wiki/Forgiveness_Rock_Record?qsrc=3044"
onmousedown="triggerActionLog('primaryContent','','center','click','primaryContent','','');"
title="Forgiveness
Rock
Record">Forgiveness
Rock
Record</a></i>.
One
of
BSS'
most
popular
songs,
&quot;Anthems
for
a
Seventeen
Year
Old
Girl&quot;,
was
sung
by
her.</p>








<p>Haines
has
also
been
a
guest
on
albums
by
artists
like
<a
href="/wiki/Stars_(Canadian_band)?qsrc=3044"
onmousedown="triggerActionLog('primaryContent','','center','click','primaryContent','','');"
title="Stars
(Canadian
band)">Stars</a>,
<a
href="/wiki/KC_Accidental?qsrc=3044"
onmousedown="triggerActionLog('primaryContent','','center','click','primaryContent','','');"
title="KC
Accidental">KC
Accidental</a>,
<a
href="/wiki/The_Stills?qsrc=3044"
onmousedown="triggerActionLog('primaryContent','','center','click','primaryContent','','');"
title="The
Stills">The
Stills</a>,
<a
href="/wiki/Jason_Collett?qsrc=3044"
onmousedown="triggerActionLog('primaryContent','','center','click','primaryContent','','');"
title="Jason
Collett">Jason
Collett</a>,
<a
href="/wiki/The_Crystal_Method?qsrc=3044"
onmousedown="triggerActionLog('primaryContent','','center','click','primaryContent','','');"
title="The
Crystal
Method">The
Crystal
Method</a>,
<a
href="/wiki/Ti%C3%ABsto?qsrc=3044"
onmousedown="triggerActionLog('primaryContent','','center','click','primaryContent','','');"
title="Ti&euml;sto">Ti&euml;sto</a>,
<a
href="/wiki/Delerium?qsrc=3044"
onmousedown="triggerActionLog('primaryContent','','center','click','primaryContent','','');"
title="Delerium">Delerium</a>,
<a
href="/wiki/K-os?qsrc=3044"
onmousedown="triggerActionLog('primaryContent','','center','click','primaryContent','','');"
title="K-os">k-os</a>,
<a
href="/wiki/MSTRKRFT?qsrc=3044"
onmousedown="triggerActionLog('primaryContent','','center','click','primaryContent','','');"
title="MSTRKRFT">MSTRKRFT</a>,
and
<a
href="/wiki/Todor_Kobakov?qsrc=3044"
onmousedown="triggerActionLog('primaryContent','','center','click','primaryContent','','');"
title="Todor
Kobakov">Todor
Kobakov</a>.</p>








<p>In
1996,
Haines
released
the
album
<i><a
href="/wiki/Cut_in_Half_and_Also_Double?qsrc=3044"
onmousedown="triggerActionLog('primaryContent','','center','click','primaryContent','','');"
title="Cut
in
Half
and
Also
Double">Cut
in
Half
and
Also
Double</a></i>.
Under
&quot;Emily
Haines
and
the
Soft
Skeleton&quot;
moniker,
she
released
in
2006
the
studio
album
<i><a
href="/wiki/Knives_Don%27t_Have_Your_Back?qsrc=3044"
onmousedown="triggerActionLog('primaryContent','','center','click','primaryContent','','');"
title="Knives
Don't
Have
Your
Back">Knives
Don't
Have
Your
Back</a></i>,
followed
in
2007
by
the
EP
<i><a
href="/wiki/What_Is_Free_to_a_Good_Home%3F?qsrc=3044"
onmousedown="triggerActionLog('primaryContent','','center','click','primaryContent','','');"
title="What
Is
Free
to
a
Good
Home?">What
Is
Free
to
a
Good
Home?</a></i>.
The
album
and
the
EP
are
a
collection
of
piano-driven
songs
backed
with
soft
strings
and
horns.
The
songs
&quot;Our
Hell&quot;
and
&quot;Doctor
Blind&quot;
were
issued
as
singles
and
also
there
were
made
music
videos
for
them.</p>








<p>In
1997,
Shaw
released
his
studio
album,
<i>Life
on
the
Clock</i>.
The
album
featured
Haines
singing
on
some
tracks.
The
songs
&quot;Down&quot;
and
&quot;Tortury&quot;
were
later
reworked
as
Metric
songs.
The
reworked
version
of
&quot;Down&quot;
featured
later
on
the
2001
EP
<i><a
href="/wiki/Static_Anonymity?qsrc=3044"
onmousedown="triggerActionLog('primaryContent','','center','click','primaryContent','','');"
title="Static
Anonymity">Static
Anonymity</a></i>
and
&quot;Tortury&quot;
(renamed
to
&quot;Torture
Me&quot;)
on
the
unreleased
version
of
<i><a
href="/wiki/Grow_Up_and_Blow_Away?qsrc=3044"
onmousedown="triggerActionLog('primaryContent','','center','click','primaryContent','','');"
title="Grow
Up
and
Blow
Away">Grow
Up
and
Blow
Away</a></i>
album.</p>








<p>Scott-Key
and
Winstead
have
their
own
side
project,
the
band
<a
href="/wiki/Bang_Lime?qsrc=3044"
onmousedown="triggerActionLog('primaryContent','','center','click','primaryContent','','');"
title="Bang
Lime">Bang
Lime</a>.
The
band
released
the
album
<i>Best
Friends
in
Love</i>
on
August
14,
2007
on
<a
href="/wiki/Last_Gang_Records?qsrc=3044"
onmousedown="triggerActionLog('primaryContent','','center','click','primaryContent','','');"
title="Last
Gang
Records">Last
Gang
Records</a>.<sup
id="cite_ref-29"
class="reference"><a
href="#cite_note-29"><span>[</span>29<span>]</span></a></sup></p>








<p>As
of
late
August
2013,
Haines
is
involved
with
FLEET4HEARme,
a
collaboration
between
herself,
Fleet
Jewelry,
and
HearMe—the
latter
is
an
organization
that
aims
to
increase
children's
access
to
music
programs
in
public
schools.
In
support
of
the
project,
Haines
explained:
&quot;I
feel
like
anybody
who
wants
to
play
an
instrument
should
be
able
to.&quot;<sup
id="cite_ref-30"
class="reference"><a
href="#cite_note-30"><span>[</span>30<span>]</span></a></sup></p>








<h2><span
class="mw-headline"
id="Music_style_and_perspectives">Music
style
and
perspectives</span>
<span
class="mw-editsection">[<a
href="/wiki?title=Metric_(band)&amp;action=edit&amp;section=9"
title="Edit
section:
Music
style
and
perspectives">edit</a>]</span></h2>








<p>Metric's
music
style
has
been
described
as
<a
href="/wiki/Indie_rock?qsrc=3044"
onmousedown="triggerActionLog('primaryContent','','center','click','primaryContent','','');"
title="Indie
rock">indie
rock</a><sup
id="cite_ref-allmusic_1-10"
class="reference"><a
href="#cite_note-allmusic-1"><span>[</span>1<span>]</span></a></sup>
and
<a
href="/wiki/Alternative_rock?qsrc=3044"
onmousedown="triggerActionLog('primaryContent','','center','click','primaryContent','','');"
title="Alternative
rock">alternative
rock</a>,<sup
id="cite_ref-allmusic_1-11"
class="reference"><a
href="#cite_note-allmusic-1"><span>[</span>1<span>]</span></a></sup>
with
elements
of
<a
href="/wiki/New_Wave_music?qsrc=3044"
onmousedown="triggerActionLog('primaryContent','','center','click','primaryContent','','');"
title="New
Wave
music"
class="mw-redirect">New
Wave</a>,<sup
id="cite_ref-allmusic_1-12"
class="reference"><a
href="#cite_note-allmusic-1"><span>[</span>1<span>]</span></a></sup>
<a
href="/wiki/Post-punk_revival?qsrc=3044"
onmousedown="triggerActionLog('primaryContent','','center','click','primaryContent','','');"
title="Post-punk
revival">post-punk
revival</a>,<sup
id="cite_ref-allmusic_1-13"
class="reference"><a
href="#cite_note-allmusic-1"><span>[</span>1<span>]</span></a></sup>
<a
href="/wiki/Synthpop?qsrc=3044"
onmousedown="triggerActionLog('primaryContent','','center','click','primaryContent','','');"
title="Synthpop">synthpop</a>,<sup
id="cite_ref-allmusic_1-14"
class="reference"><a
href="#cite_note-allmusic-1"><span>[</span>1<span>]</span></a></sup>
<a
href="/wiki/Dance-rock?qsrc=3044"
onmousedown="triggerActionLog('primaryContent','','center','click','primaryContent','','');"
title="Dance-rock">dance-rock</a>.<sup
id="cite_ref-allmusic_1-15"
class="reference"><a
href="#cite_note-allmusic-1"><span>[</span>1<span>]</span></a></sup>
Sounds
generated
by
<a
href="/wiki/Synthesizers?qsrc=3044"
onmousedown="triggerActionLog('primaryContent','','center','click','primaryContent','','');"
title="Synthesizers"
class="mw-redirect">synthesizers</a>
are
prominent
in
their
songs.</p>








<p>Their
sound
evolved
from
the
mellow/<a
href="/wiki/Downtempo?qsrc=3044"
onmousedown="triggerActionLog('primaryContent','','center','click','primaryContent','','');"
title="Downtempo">downtempo</a>
style
of
their
early
EPs
and
<i><a
href="/wiki/Grow_Up_and_Blow_Away?qsrc=3044"
onmousedown="triggerActionLog('primaryContent','','center','click','primaryContent','','');"
title="Grow
Up
and
Blow
Away">Grow
Up
and
Blow
Away</a></i>
album,
to
the
<a
href="/wiki/New_wave_music?qsrc=3044"
onmousedown="triggerActionLog('primaryContent','','center','click','primaryContent','','');"
title="New
wave
music">new
wave</a>
style
of
<i><a
href="/wiki/Old_World_Underground,_Where_Are_You_Now%3F?qsrc=3044"
onmousedown="triggerActionLog('primaryContent','','center','click','primaryContent','','');"
title="Old
World
Underground,
Where
Are
You
Now?">Old
World
Underground,
Where
Are
You
Now?</a></i>,
then
more
<a
href="/wiki/Hard_rock?qsrc=3044"
onmousedown="triggerActionLog('primaryContent','','center','click','primaryContent','','');"
title="Hard
rock">hard
rock</a>
on
<i><a
href="/wiki/Live_It_Out?qsrc=3044"
onmousedown="triggerActionLog('primaryContent','','center','click','primaryContent','','');"
title="Live
It
Out">Live
It
Out</a></i>,
then
to
the
accessible
<a
href="/wiki/Indie_rock?qsrc=3044"
onmousedown="triggerActionLog('primaryContent','','center','click','primaryContent','','');"
title="Indie
rock">indie
rock</a>
of
<i><a
href="/wiki/Fantasies_(album)?qsrc=3044"
onmousedown="triggerActionLog('primaryContent','','center','click','primaryContent','','');"
title="Fantasies
(album)">Fantasies</a></i>,
and
finally
to
the
more
<a
href="/wiki/Electronic_music?qsrc=3044"
onmousedown="triggerActionLog('primaryContent','','center','click','primaryContent','','');"
title="Electronic
music">electronic</a>
<i><a
href="/wiki/Synthetica?qsrc=3044"
onmousedown="triggerActionLog('primaryContent','','center','click','primaryContent','','');"
title="Synthetica">Synthetica</a></i>.
Some
of
their
songs
(like
&quot;IOU&quot;,
&quot;Succexy&quot;,
&quot;<a
href="/wiki/Combat_Baby?qsrc=3044"
onmousedown="triggerActionLog('primaryContent','','center','click','primaryContent','','');"
title="Combat
Baby"
class="mw-redirect">Combat
Baby</a>&quot;,
&quot;<a
href="/wiki/Monster_Hospital?qsrc=3044"
onmousedown="triggerActionLog('primaryContent','','center','click','primaryContent','','');"
title="Monster
Hospital">Monster
Hospital</a>&quot;)
include
anti-<a
href="/wiki/War?qsrc=3044"
onmousedown="triggerActionLog('primaryContent','','center','click','primaryContent','','');"
title="War">war</a>
messages.<sup
id="cite_ref-31"
class="reference"><a
href="#cite_note-31"><span>[</span>31<span>]</span></a></sup><sup
id="cite_ref-32"
class="reference"><a
href="#cite_note-32"><span>[</span>32<span>]</span></a></sup><sup
id="cite_ref-33"
class="reference"><a
href="#cite_note-33"><span>[</span>33<span>]</span></a></sup></p>








<p>The
band
also
recorded
many
covers
from
artists
like
<a
href="/wiki/Bob_Dylan?qsrc=3044"
onmousedown="triggerActionLog('primaryContent','','center','click','primaryContent','','');"
title="Bob
Dylan">Bob
Dylan</a>,
<a
href="/wiki/Pink_Floyd?qsrc=3044"
onmousedown="triggerActionLog('primaryContent','','center','click','primaryContent','','');"
title="Pink
Floyd">Pink
Floyd</a>,
<a
href="/wiki/Pet_Shop_Boys?qsrc=3044"
onmousedown="triggerActionLog('primaryContent','','center','click','primaryContent','','');"
title="Pet
Shop
Boys">Pet
Shop
Boys</a>,
<a
href="/wiki/The_Church_(band)?qsrc=3044"
onmousedown="triggerActionLog('primaryContent','','center','click','primaryContent','','');"
title="The
Church
(band)">The
Church</a>,
<a
href="/wiki/Death_from_Above_1979?qsrc=3044"
onmousedown="triggerActionLog('primaryContent','','center','click','primaryContent','','');"
title="Death
from
Above
1979">Death
from
Above
1979</a>,
<a
href="/wiki/Brenda_Lee?qsrc=3044"
onmousedown="triggerActionLog('primaryContent','','center','click','primaryContent','','');"
title="Brenda
Lee">Brenda
Lee</a>,
<a
href="/wiki/Tom_Waits?qsrc=3044"
onmousedown="triggerActionLog('primaryContent','','center','click','primaryContent','','');"
title="Tom
Waits">Tom
Waits</a>,
<a
href="/wiki/Neil_Young?qsrc=3044"
onmousedown="triggerActionLog('primaryContent','','center','click','primaryContent','','');"
title="Neil
Young">Neil
Young</a>,
<a
href="/wiki/Blondie_(band)?qsrc=3044"
onmousedown="triggerActionLog('primaryContent','','center','click','primaryContent','','');"
title="Blondie
(band)">Blondie</a>,
<a
href="/wiki/The_Strokes?qsrc=3044"
onmousedown="triggerActionLog('primaryContent','','center','click','primaryContent','','');"
title="The
Strokes">The
Strokes</a>,
<a
href="/wiki/Morrissey?qsrc=3044"
onmousedown="triggerActionLog('primaryContent','','center','click','primaryContent','','');"
title="Morrissey">Morrissey</a>
and
<a
href="/wiki/Elliott_Smith?qsrc=3044"
onmousedown="triggerActionLog('primaryContent','','center','click','primaryContent','','');"
title="Elliott
Smith">Elliott
Smith</a>.
They
also
released
many
<a
href="/wiki/Acoustic_music?qsrc=3044"
onmousedown="triggerActionLog('primaryContent','','center','click','primaryContent','','');"
title="Acoustic
music">acoustic</a>
versions
of
some
of
their
own
songs
on
deluxe
versions
of
some
of
their
albums.<sup
class="Template-Fact"
style="white-space:nowrap;">[<i><a
href="http://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Wikipedia:Citation_needed"
target="_blank"
title="Wikipedia:Citation
needed"><span
title="This
claim
needs
references
to
reliable
sources.
(August
2013)">citation
needed</span></a></i>]</sup></p>

class="mw-headline"

<span

<p>Metric
is
known
as
one
of
today's
best
live
rock
bands.<sup
id="cite_ref-34"
class="reference"><a
href="#cite_note-34"><span>[</span>34<span>]</span></a></sup><sup
id="cite_ref-35"
class="reference"><a
href="#cite_note-35"><span>[</span>35<span>]</span></a></sup>
They've
toured
mostly
in
<a
href="/wiki/North_America?qsrc=3044"
onmousedown="triggerActionLog('primaryContent','','center','click','primaryContent','','');"
title="North
America">North
America</a>,
<a
href="/wiki/South_America?qsrc=3044"
onmousedown="triggerActionLog('primaryContent','','center','click','primaryContent','','');"
title="South
America">South
America</a>
and
<a
href="/wiki/Europe?qsrc=3044"
onmousedown="triggerActionLog('primaryContent','','center','click','primaryContent','','');"
title="Europe">Europe</a>,
but
also
have
toured
through
Australia,
The
Philippines,
and
Japan.<sup
id="cite_ref-lastfm_36-0"
class="reference"><a
href="#cite_note-lastfm-36"><span>[</span>36<span>]</span></a></sup></p>








<p>During
Metric
live
performances,
<a
href="/wiki/Emily_Haines?qsrc=3044"
onmousedown="triggerActionLog('primaryContent','','center','click','primaryContent','','');"
title="Emily
Haines">Emily
Haines</a>
sings
and
play
two
<a
href="/wiki/Synthesizers?qsrc=3044"
onmousedown="triggerActionLog('primaryContent','','center','click','primaryContent','','');"
title="Synthesizers"
class="mw-redirect">synthesizers</a>
and
occasionally
she
plays
a
<a
href="/wiki/Tambourine?qsrc=3044"
onmousedown="triggerActionLog('primaryContent','','center','click','primaryContent','','');"
title="Tambourine">tambourine</a>
or
a
<a
href="/wiki/Electric_guitar?qsrc=3044"
onmousedown="triggerActionLog('primaryContent','','center','click','primaryContent','','');"
title="Electric
guitar">guitar</a>.
One
of
the
two
synthesizers
is
a
<a
href="/wiki/Sequential_Circuits?qsrc=3044"
onmousedown="triggerActionLog('primaryContent','','center','click','primaryContent','','');"
title="Sequential
Circuits">Sequential
Circuits</a>
Pro-One,<sup
id="cite_ref-37"
class="reference"><a
href="#cite_note-37"><span>[</span>37<span>]</span></a></sup>
which
she
has
played
at
every
live
performance
with
the
whole
band
since
<i><a
href="/wiki/Old_World_Underground,_Where_Are_You_Now%3F?qsrc=3044"
onmousedown="triggerActionLog('primaryContent','','center','click','primaryContent','','');"
title="Old
World
Underground,
Where
Are
You
Now?">Old
World
Underground</a></i>
era.
Her
other
keyboard
is
a
<a
href="/wiki/Nord_Wave?qsrc=3044"
onmousedown="triggerActionLog('primaryContent','','center','click','primaryContent','','');"
title="Nord
Wave">Nord</a>
Wave
with
a
custom
built
stand.
<a
href="/wiki/James_Shaw_(musician)?qsrc=3044"
onmousedown="triggerActionLog('primaryContent','','center','click','primaryContent','','');"
title="James
Shaw
(musician)">James
Shaw</a>
plays
<a
href="/wiki/Electric_guitar?qsrc=3044"
onmousedown="triggerActionLog('primaryContent','','center','click','primaryContent','','');"
title="Electric
guitar">guitar</a>
and
Joshua
Winstead
plays
<a
href="/wiki/Bass_guitar?qsrc=3044"
onmousedown="triggerActionLog('primaryContent','','center','click','primaryContent','','');"
title="Bass
guitar">bass</a>.
Both
Shaw
and
Winstead
occasionally
play
a
synthesizer
each,
and
also
sing
<a
href="/wiki/Backing_vocals?qsrc=3044"
onmousedown="triggerActionLog('primaryContent','','center','click','primaryContent','','');"
title="Backing
vocals"
class="mw-redirect">backing
vocals</a>.
Joules
Scott-Key
plays
drums.</p>








<p>The
band
is
also
known
for
their
<a
href="/wiki/Acoustic_music?qsrc=3044"
onmousedown="triggerActionLog('primaryContent','','center','click','primaryContent','','');"
title="Acoustic
music">acoustic</a>
performances
as
a
duo,
with
<a
href="/wiki/Emily_Haines?qsrc=3044"
onmousedown="triggerActionLog('primaryContent','','center','click','primaryContent','','');"
title="Emily
Haines">Emily
Haines</a>
singing
and/or
playing
various
instruments
(<a
href="/wiki/Piano?qsrc=3044"
onmousedown="triggerActionLog('primaryContent','','center','click','primaryContent','','');"
title="Piano">piano</a>,
<a
href="/wiki/Harmonica?qsrc=3044"
onmousedown="triggerActionLog('primaryContent','','center','click','primaryContent','','');"
title="Harmonica">harmonica</a>,
<a
href="/wiki/Tambourine?qsrc=3044"
onmousedown="triggerActionLog('primaryContent','','center','click','primaryContent','','');"
title="Tambourine">tambourine</a>)
and
<a
href="/wiki/James_Shaw_(musician)?qsrc=3044"
onmousedown="triggerActionLog('primaryContent','','center','click','primaryContent','','');"
title="James
Shaw
(musician)">James
Shaw</a>
playing
the
<a
href="/wiki/Acoustic_guitar?qsrc=3044"
onmousedown="triggerActionLog('primaryContent','','center','click','primaryContent','','');"
title="Acoustic
guitar">acoustic
guitar</a>
and
occasionally
singing.</p>








<p>Metric
has
performed
at
many
well
known
music
festivals
around
the
world
like
Coachella,
Osheaga,
Bluesfest,
Pemberton,
All
Points

Glastonbury,

Virgin
Festival,
Download
Festival,

Squamish,

Sasquatch!,
La
Route
Du
Rock,
The
Great
Escape,
Edgefest,
Reading
and
Leeds
Festival,
Rock
Werchter,
Wireless,
Splendour
in
the
Grass,
Lollapalooza,
Austin
City
Limits,
and
the
Hillside
Festival.<sup
id="cite_ref-lastfm_36-1"
class="reference"><a
href="#cite_note-lastfm-36"><span>[</span>36<span>]</span></a></sup></p>

guitar,
tambourine,
harmonica,
piano

Shaw</a>&nbsp;–

and

guitars,
synthesizers,
theremin,
backing
vocals
(1998–present)</li>

Winstead&nbsp;–
bass
guitar,
synthesizers,
backing
vocals
(2001–present)</li>









<li>Joules
Scott-Key&nbsp;–
drums,
percussion
(2001–present)</li>








</ul>

=
5;
























window['backfillParam']['pl_tnum']
=
count;












window['backfillParam']['pl_bnum']
=
countBottom;








}


































var
_matchUrl
=
"/afc-match?q=Metric_%28band%29&page=1&ac=24&qid=A1673DA2BB5DDF9AE8864ADEBBCED40C&qsrc=121&dm=&qrt=2&lid="+
"&o=0&l=dir&oo=&cl=ca-aj-cat&ch=cx_ask_wiki,ad_dirN";





















_matchUrl+=
"&userip=76.78.3.114";




































_matchUrl+="&losid=a&locid=encw&lodid=us&loaid=a16";









var
location
=
window.location
+
"";








location
=
location.substring(7);








var
cutIdx
=
location.indexOf("/");








if
(location.indexOf(":")
>
-1)
{




















cutIdx
=
1
+
cutIdx
+
location.substring(cutIdx+1).indexOf("/");








}









var
urlPrefix
=
location.substring(0,
cutIdx);








_matchUrl
=
"http://"
+
urlPrefix
+
_matchUrl
+
"&afcec="
+
count
+
"&afcecb="
+
countBottom;








ajax_get(_matchUrl,
null,
null);




}





function
getXHR()
{








if
(window.XMLHttpRequest)
{












return
new
XMLHttpRequest();








}
else
if
(window.ActiveXObject)
{












try
{
















return
new
ActiveXObject("Msxml2.XMLHTTP");












}
catch
(e)
{
















try
{




















return
new
ActiveXObject("Microsoft.XMLHTTP");
















}
catch
(E)
{




















return
null;
















}












}








}








else
{












return
null;








}




}





function
ajax_get(url,
onsuccess,
onerror)
{








var
obj
=
getXHR();








if(obj)
{












obj.onreadystatechange
=
function()
{
















if(obj.readyState==4)
{




















if
(obj.status
==
200
&&
typeof(onsuccess)
==
"function")
{
























onsuccess(obj);




















}
else
if
(typeof(onerror)
==
"function")
{
























onerror(obj);




















}






















try
{
























delete
obj['onreadystatechange'];




















}
catch(e)
{}
















}












};












obj.open("GET",
url,
true,
"",
"");












obj.send(null);












return
obj;








}
else
{












if(onerror)
{
















onerror("Error
creating
XHR");












}
else
{
















a10.debug("Error
creating
XHR");












}












return
null;








}




}





afc_match();

</script>
